## Run-Level Observations
- Current selected set is a Park Plaza slice: 14 brand URLs, 457 hotel/property URLs, 78 meeting-event URLs, and 7 offer URLs.

- 0 selected URLs returned HTTP 200 useful HTML without the access-restricted template.
